3785
3786struct MipsGenMCSubtargetInfo : public MCSubtargetInfo {
3787 MipsGenMCSubtargetInfo(const Triple &TT,
3788 StringRef CPU, StringRef TuneCPU, StringRef FS,
3789 ArrayRef<SubtargetFeatureKV> PF,
3790 ArrayRef<SubtargetSubTypeKV> PD,
3791 const MCWriteProcResEntry *WPR,
3792 const MCWriteLatencyEntry *WL,
3793 const MCReadAdvanceEntry *RA, const InstrStage *IS,
3794 const unsigned *OC, const unsigned *FP) :
3795 MCSubtargetInfo(TT, CPU, TuneCPU, FS, PF, PD,
3796 WPR, WL, RA, IS, OC, FP) { }
3797
3798 unsigned resolveVariantSchedClass(unsigned SchedClass,
3799 const MCInst *MI, const MCInstrInfo *MCII,
3800 unsigned CPUID) const override {
3801 return Mips_MC::resolveVariantSchedClassImpl(SchedClass, MI, MCII, CPUID);
3802 }
3803};
3804
3805static inline MCSubtargetInfo *createMipsMCSubtargetInfoImpl(const Triple &TT, StringRef CPU, StringRef TuneCPU, StringRef FS) {
3806 return new MipsGenMCSubtargetInfo(TT, CPU, TuneCPU, FS, MipsFeatureKV, MipsSubTypeKV,
3807 MipsWriteProcResTable, MipsWriteLatencyTable, MipsReadAdvanceTable,
3808 nullptr, nullptr, nullptr);
3809}

3819#include "llvm/Support/Debug.h"
3820#include "llvm/Support/raw_ostream.h"
3821
3822// ParseSubtargetFeatures - Parses features string setting specified
3823// subtarget options.
3824void llvm::MipsSubtarget::ParseSubtargetFeatures(StringRef CPU, StringRef TuneCPU, StringRef FS) {
3825 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "\nFeatures:" << FS);
3826 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "\nCPU:" << CPU);
3827 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "\nTuneCPU:" << TuneCPU << "\n\n");
3828 InitMCProcessorInfo(CPU, TuneCPU, FS);
3829 const FeatureBitset &Bits = getFeatureBits();
3830 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureAbs2008]) Abs2008 = true;
3831 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureCRC]) HasCRC = true;
3832 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureCnMips]) HasCnMips = true;
3833 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureCnMipsP]) HasCnMipsP = true;
3834 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureDSP]) HasDSP = true;
3835 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureDSPR2]) HasDSPR2 = true;
3836 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureDSPR3]) HasDSPR3 = true;
3837 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureEVA]) HasEVA = true;
3838 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureFP64Bit]) IsFP64bit = true;
3839 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureFPXX]) IsFPXX = true;
3840 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureGINV]) HasGINV = true;
3841 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureGP64Bit]) IsGP64bit = true;
3842 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureLongCalls]) UseLongCalls = true;
3843 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMSA]) HasMSA = true;
3844 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMT]) HasMT = true;
3845 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMicroMips]) InMicroMipsMode = true;
3846 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips1] && MipsArchVersion < Mips1) MipsArchVersion = Mips1;
3847 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips2] && MipsArchVersion < Mips2) MipsArchVersion = Mips2;
3848 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips3] && MipsArchVersion < Mips3) MipsArchVersion = Mips3;
3849 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips3D]) Has3D = true;
3850 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips3_32]) HasMips3_32 = true;
3851 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips3_32r2]) HasMips3_32r2 = true;
3852 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips4] && MipsArchVersion < Mips4) MipsArchVersion = Mips4;
3853 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips4_32]) HasMips4_32 = true;
3854 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips4_32r2]) HasMips4_32r2 = true;
3855 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips5] && MipsArchVersion < Mips5) MipsArchVersion = Mips5;
3856 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips5_32r2]) HasMips5_32r2 = true;
3857 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips16]) InMips16Mode = true;
3858 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips32] && MipsArchVersion < Mips32) MipsArchVersion = Mips32;
3859 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips32r2] && MipsArchVersion < Mips32r2) MipsArchVersion = Mips32r2;
3860 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips32r3] && MipsArchVersion < Mips32r3) MipsArchVersion = Mips32r3;
3861 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips32r5] && MipsArchVersion < Mips32r5) MipsArchVersion = Mips32r5;
3862 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips32r6] && MipsArchVersion < Mips32r6) MipsArchVersion = Mips32r6;
3863 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips64] && MipsArchVersion < Mips64) MipsArchVersion = Mips64;
3864 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips64r2] && MipsArchVersion < Mips64r2) MipsArchVersion = Mips64r2;
3865 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips64r3] && MipsArchVersion < Mips64r3) MipsArchVersion = Mips64r3;
3866 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips64r5] && MipsArchVersion < Mips64r5) MipsArchVersion = Mips64r5;
3867 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureMips64r6] && MipsArchVersion < Mips64r6) MipsArchVersion = Mips64r6;
3868 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureNaN2008]) IsNaN2008bit = true;
3869 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureNoABICalls]) NoABICalls = true;
3870 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureNoMadd4]) DisableMadd4 = true;
3871 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureNoOddSPReg]) UseOddSPReg = false;
3872 if (Bits[Mips::FeaturePTR64Bit]) IsPTR64bit = true;
3873 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureSingleFloat]) IsSingleFloat = true;
3874 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureSoftFloat]) IsSoftFloat = true;
3875 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureSym32]) HasSym32 = true;
3876 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureUseIndirectJumpsHazard]) UseIndirectJumpsHazard = true;
3877 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureUseTCCInDIV]) UseTCCInDIV = false;
3878 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureVFPU]) HasVFPU = true;
3879 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureVirt]) HasVirt = true;
3880 if (Bits[Mips::FeatureXGOT]) UseXGOT = true;
3881 if (Bits[Mips::ImplP5600] && ProcImpl < MipsSubtarget::CPU::P5600) ProcImpl = MipsSubtarget::CPU::P5600;
3882}
